<content>
1: # TrulyFreeOCR Project Review
2: 
3: ## Overview
4: **TrulyFreeOCR** is a commercially-safe OCR pipeline designed to process non-searchable PDFs and output fully searchable, MRC-compressed (Mixed Raster Content) PDFs. It is tailored for commercial and enterprise teams by strictly relying on permissive licenses (Apache 2.0, BSD, MIT) and operating entirely offline (CPU-only, no GPUs).
5: 
6: ### Core Components & Pipeline
7: 1. **PageExtractor**: Uses PDFBox to render PDF pages into `BufferedImage` at a specified DPI (default 300).
8: 2. **ImageSegmenter**: Performs pure-Java page segmentation (grayscale conversion -> tile-based background normalization -> Otsu binarization -> inpainting) to separate the clean background from the text layer.
9: 3. **OCREngine**: Wraps the Tesseract CLI to extract word-level bounding boxes and text from the images. 
10: 4. **JBIG2Compressor**: Designed to compress foreground text masks efficiently.
11: 5. **PDFAssembler**: Re-assembles the PDF with three layers: a clean background, a stencil mask for text, and an invisible, searchable text layer.
12: 6. **MetadataPreserver**: Copies metadata (bookmarks, outlines, XMP) from the source to the output PDF.
13: 
14: ## Evaluation & Performance
15: Based on the `Evaluation.md` data:
16: - **Accuracy**: It performs exceptionally well on standard prose (Word Error Rate of 0.9%–3.2% and Character Error Rate of 0.2%–1.2%). Word recall and precision are very high (>98%).
17: - **Edge Cases**: Non-standard layouts (e.g., multi-column, mixed languages, or heavy punctuation) result in a sharp drop in accuracy, inflating the aggregate WER to ~60-70%.
18: - **Speed**: The pipeline is quite slow on a single thread (~85 seconds per page at 300 DPI). While linear scaling is expected, this makes it computationally expensive for very large documents.
19: 
20: ---
21: 
22: ## Resolved Issues (Fixed in Recent Commits)
23: 
24: 1. **Out-Of-Memory (OOM) Vulnerability (Fixed)**: The pipeline now successfully streams pages. Images are flushed from memory after they are temporarily written to disk, ensuring memory usage stays flat regardless of page count.
25: 2. **Subprocess Deadlock (Fixed)**: `SubprocessRunner.java` now properly drains `stdout` and `stderr` in separate daemon threads concurrently with `process.waitFor()`, avoiding deadlocks caused by filled OS pipe buffers.
26: 3. **Cumulative Text Matrix Drift (Fixed)**: OCR text is correctly placed using absolute offsets (`setTextMatrix(Matrix.getTranslateInstance(x, y))`), eliminating horizontal drifting.
27: 4. **Concurrency CLI Flag Logic Flaw (Fixed)**: The `--threads` flag logic correctly respects the `pipeline.ocr.maxThreads` limit.
28: 5. **Naive JSONC Parsing Bug (Fixed)**: The settings parser safely handles `//` within strings.
29: 
30: ---
31: 
32: ## Remaining Bugs (Third Pass)
33: 
34: While the OOM and Deadlock issues have been robustly handled, the **JBIG2 Integration is still fundamentally broken** in multiple ways. Despite adding the batch processing logic for `-p`, two critical bugs guarantee it will either fail silently or artificially bloat your PDF.
35: 
36: ### 1. The `jbig2enc` Basename Flag (`-b`) is Missing (Critical Functional Bug)
37: In `JBIG2Compressor.java`, the `compressAllFromDir()` method calls `jbig2enc -p -s mask-0.png mask-1.png ...` without providing a basename (`-b`).
38: - **The Problem:** Without the `-b` flag, `jbig2enc` defaults to outputting files named `output.sym`, `output.0000`, `output.0001` in the current working directory. However, your Java code looks for `[tempDir]/mask-0.sym` and `[tempDir]/mask-0.jbig2`.
39: - **The Impact:** Because it searches for filenames that `jbig2enc` never created, `symFile.exists()` evaluates to `false`. The batch JBIG2 process returns `null`, and the PDFAssembler silently falls back to CCITT G4 compression every single time.
40: - **Fix:** You must pass `-b <basename>` (e.g., `-b temp/page`) to `jbig2enc` so you can deterministically read `temp/page.sym` and `temp/page.0000`.
41: 
42: ### 2. PDFBox Shared Global Stream Duplication (Performance / Architectural Bug)
43: In `PDFAssembler.java`, you now create the `JBIG2Globals` stream to share the global dictionary.
44: - **The Problem:** In `addPageJbig2`, which is called inside a loop for *every page*, you do this:
45:   ```java
46:   COSStream globalsStream = doc.getDocument().createCOSStream();
47:   os.write(globalSym);
48:   img.getCOSObject().setItem(COSName.JBIG2_GLOBALS, globalsStream);
49:   ```
50: - **The Impact:** Even when the previous bug is fixed, you are creating a **brand new `COSStream` object** containing the exact same `globalSym` byte array for *every single page*. PDFBox does not deduplicate streams automatically. If you have 500 pages, the global dictionary is embedded 500 times in the PDF, totally destroying the file-size advantage of the global dictionary.
51: - **Fix:** You must create the `globalsStream` **once** per `PDDocument` (e.g., cache it as an instance variable in `PDFAssembler` or pass it as an object), and then reuse that exact same `COSStream` reference for every `PDImageXObject`.
52: 
53: ### 3. Hardcoded Page Dimensions for Batch JBIG2 (Minor Bug)
54: In `TrulyFreeOCR.java` (lines 177-180), you capture `imgWidth` and `imgHeight` exclusively from page 0, and then apply those dimensions to every mask in the JBIG2 batch result (`CompressionResult`).
55: - **The Problem:** PDFs can contain mixed page sizes (e.g., a mix of US Letter and Legal). If a later page has different dimensions, it will be rendered with the incorrect width/height taken from page 0.
56: - **Fix:** Capture the dimensions of each page individually and pass them in a list or array to `compressAllFromDir()`, mapping them correctly to the output `CompressionResult`.

(End of file - total 56 lines)
</content>
```

<details>
<summary>Thinking</summary>

The reviewer found 3 remaining bugs:

1. **Missing `-b` flag in `jbig2enc` call**: `compressAllFromDir()` calls `jbig2enc -p -s mask-0.png mask-1.png ...` without `-b <basename>`, so `jbig2enc` outputs `output.sym` and `output.0000` files, but the Java code looks for `mask-0.sym` / `mask-0.jbig2`. The fix is to pass `-b` to `jbig2enc`.

2. **Global stream duplication**: `addPageJbig2` creates a new `COSStream` for `JBIG2Globals` on every page. The fix is to cache the globals stream once in PDFAssembler.

3. **Hardcoded page dimensions**: `imgWidth` and `imgHeight` are captured only from page 0 and applied to all pages. The fix is to capture per-page dimensions.

Let me verify these by reading the relevant code:

Bug 1: Let me read `JBIG2Compressor.compressAllFromDir()`.
Bug 2: Let me read `PDFAssembler.addPageJbig2()` and `createJbig2ImageXObject()`.
Bug 3: Let me read `TrulyFreeOCR.java` lines around 177-180.

Actually, I already read `addPageJbig2` and `createJbig2ImageXObject` — the globals stream is indeed created per-page inside `createJbig2ImageXObject`. I need to cache it.

Let me read the other files.

</details>

87:      * Compresses foreground mask PNGs in a single jbig2enc invocation
88:      * with the {@code -p} flag, producing one shared symbol dictionary
89:      * and per-page JBIG2 streams.
90:      *
91:      * @param maskDir    Directory containing mask PNGs named {@code mask-0.png},
92:      *                   {@code mask-1.png}, ..., {@code mask-{pageCount-1}.png}.
93:      * @param pageCount  Number of masks / pages.
94:      * @param imgWidth   Width of each mask in pixels.
95:      * @param imgHeight  Height of each mask in pixels.
96:      * @return BatchResult with shared global sym and per-page data, or null if
97:      *         jbig2enc is unavailable or fails (caller should use CCITT fallback).
98:      */
99:     public BatchResult compressAllFromDir(File maskDir, int pageCount, int imgWidth, int imgHeight) throws IOException {
100:         File jbig2enc = findJbig2enc();
101:         if (jbig2enc == null) return null;
102: 
103:         List<String> pngPaths = new ArrayList<>(pageCount);
104:         for (int i = 0; i < pageCount; i++) {
105:             pngPaths.add(new File(maskDir, "mask-" + i + ".png").getAbsolutePath());
106:         }
107: 
108:         String flags = Settings.getInstance().getString("jbig2enc.flags", "-p -s");
109:         List<String> args = new ArrayList<>();
110:         for (String f : flags.split("\\s+")) {
111:             if (!f.isEmpty()) args.add(f);
112:         }
113:         args.addAll(pngPaths);
114: 
115:         SubprocessRunner.Result result = SubprocessRunner.run(jbig2enc, args, -1);
116:         if (result.getExitCode() != 0) return null;
117: 
118:         // jbig2enc writes output files alongside the first input file
119:         String firstPng = pngPaths.get(0);
120:         String prefix = firstPng.replaceAll("\\.png$", "");
121:         File symFile = new File(prefix + ".sym");
122:         byte[] globalSym = symFile.exists() ? Files.readAllBytes(symFile.toPath()) : new byte[0];
123:         if (globalSym.length == 0) return null;
124: 
125:         List<CompressionResult> pages = new ArrayList<>(pageCount);
126:         for (int i = 0; i < pageCount; i++) {

128:             String pfx = pngPath.replaceAll("\\.png$", "");
129:             File pageFile = new File(pfx + ".jbig2");
130:             byte[] pageData = pageFile.exists() ? Files.readAllBytes(pageFile.toPath()) : new byte[0];
131:             pages.add(new CompressionResult(pageData, imgWidth, imgHeight, true));
132:         }
133: 
134:         return new BatchResult(globalSym, pages);
135:     }
136: 
137:     /**
138:      * Attempts JBIG2 compression via jbig2enc; falls back to CCITT G4 on failure.
139:      *
140:      * @param foregroundMask  Binary image (TYPE_BYTE_BINARY, black=foreground).
141:      * @return CompressionResult with either JBIG2 or CCITT G4 data.
142:      */
143:     public CompressionResult compress(BufferedImage foregroundMask) throws IOException {
144:         File jbig2enc = findJbig2enc();
145:         if (jbig2enc != null) {
146:             try {
147:                 return compressWithJbig2enc(jbig2enc, foregroundMask);
148:             } catch (IOException e) {
149:                 // jbig2enc failed → fall through to fallback
150:             }
151:         }
152:         return compressWithFallback(foregroundMask);
153:     }
154: 
155:     /**
156:      * Locates the jbig2enc binary for the current OS.
157:      *
158:      * Searches native/{os}/jbig2enc (or jbig2enc.exe on Windows).
159:      * The base path can be overridden via system property "tfocr.native.dir"
160:      * (defaults to "native").
161:      *
162:      * @return The executable File, or null if not found.
163:      */
164:     private File findJbig2enc() {
165:         Os os = PlatformUtils.detectOs();
166:         String dirName;
167:         switch (os) {
168:             case WINDOWS: dirName = "win"; break;
169:             case MAC: dirName = "mac"; break;
170:             default: dirName = "linux";
171:         }
172:         File exe = new File(nativeDir + "/" + dirName, os == Os.WINDOWS ? "jbig2enc.exe" : "jbig2enc");
173:         if (exe.canExecute()) return exe;
174:         return null;
175:     }
176: 
177:     /**
178:      * Runs jbig2enc and concatenates global sym + page jbig2 into one byte array.
179:      *
180:      * PDF JBIG2Decode streams require global segments (symbol dictionary)
181:      * followed by page data — exactly the .sym + .jbig2 layout that
182:      * jbig2enc produces.
183:      */
184:     private CompressionResult compressWithJbig2enc(File jbig2enc, BufferedImage mask) throws IOException {
185:         File tempPng = File.createTempFile("tfocr-jbig2-", ".png");
186:         tempPng.deleteOnExit();
187:         javax.imageio.ImageIO.write(mask, "png", tempPng);
188: 
189:         try {
190:             String prefix = tempPng.getAbsolutePath().replaceAll("\\.png$", "");
191: 
192:             String flags = Settings.getInstance().getString("jbig2enc.flags", "-p -s");
193:             java.util.List<String> args = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
194:             for (String f : flags.split("\\s+")) {
195:                 if (!f.isEmpty()) args.add(f);
196:             }
197:             args.add(tempPng.getAbsolutePath());
198: 
199:             SubprocessRunner.Result result = SubprocessRunner.run(jbig2enc, args, -1);
200:             if (result.getExitCode() != 0) {
201:                 throw new IOException("jbig2enc failed: " + result.getStderrString());
202:             }
203: 
204:             File symFile = new File(prefix + ".sym");
205:             File jbig2File = new File(prefix + ".jbig2");
206: 
207:             byte[] symData = symFile.exists() ? java.nio.file.Files.readAllBytes(symFile.toPath()) : new byte[0];
208:             byte[] jbig2Data = jbig2File.exists() ? java.nio.file.Files.readAllBytes(jbig2File.toPath()) : new byte[0];
209: 
210:             byte[] combined = new byte[symData.length + jbig2Data.length];
211:             System.arraycopy(symData, 0, combined, 0, symData.length);
212:             System.arraycopy(jbig2Data, 0, combined, symData.length, jbig2Data.length);
213: 
214:             return new CompressionResult(combined, mask.getWidth(), mask.getHeight(), true);
215:         } finally {
216:             String prefix = tempPng.getAbsolutePath().replaceAll("\\.png$", "");
217:             for (String ext : new String[]{".png", ".sym", ".jbig2"}) {
218:                 File f = new File(prefix + ext);
219:                 if (f.exists()) f.delete();
220:             }
221:         }
222:     }
223: 
224:     /**
225:      * Fallback: encodes the mask as CCITT Group 4 fax using PDFBox's CCITTFactory.
226:      */
227:     private CompressionResult compressWithFallback(BufferedImage mask) throws IOException {
228:         // Create a throwaway PDDocument to use CCITTFactory
229:         try (PDDocument doc = new PDDocument()) {
230:             PDImageXObject ccitt = CCITTFactory.createFromImage(doc, mask);
231:             return new CompressionResult(extractStreamBytes(ccitt), mask.getWidth(), mask.getHeight(), false);
232:         }
233:     }
234: 
235:     private static byte[] extractStreamBytes(PDImageXObject image) throws IOException {
236:         try (java.io.InputStream is = image.createInputStream()) {
237:             return is.readAllBytes();
238:         }
239:     }
240: }

35: /**
36:  * Re-assembles a searchable PDF from per-page inputs:
37:  *   - Source PDF (copied for page dimensions / media boxes)
38:  *   - Cleaned background images
39:  *   - Binary foreground masks (CCITT G4 compressed stencil overlay)
40:  *   - OCR results (invisible text layer)
41:  *
42:  * MRC-like layout (per page):
43:  *   1. Background layer: cleaned page image (Lossless PNG for now).
44:  *   2. Foreground mask: CCITT G4 compressed binary mask, drawn as a
45:  *      PDF ImageMask stencil in black — reveals only the text pixels
46:  *      on top of the background.
47:  *   3. Text layer: invisible OCR text (RenderingMode.NEITHER = Tr 3),
48:  *      selectable and searchable but not visible.
49:  *
50:  * Rendering mode NEITHER makes text invisible on screen/print while
51:  * keeping it selectable and searchable.
52:  *
53:  * Coordinate transformation:
54:  *   Page images at 300 DPI → PDF user space at 72 DPI.
55:  *   scaleX = pageWidth_pts  / imageWidth_px
56:  *   scaleY = pageHeight_pts / imageHeight_px
57:  *   Y is flipped: image origin is top-left, PDF origin is bottom-left.
58:  */
59: public class PDFAssembler {
60: 
61:     private final PDType1Font font;
62:     private final float minFontSize;
63:     private final MetadataPreserver preserver = new MetadataPreserver();
64:     private File pdfaFontFile;
65:     private JBIG2Compressor compressor;
66: 
67:     public PDFAssembler() {
68:         this("HELVETICA", 1f);
69:     }
70: 
71:     public PDFAssembler(String fontName, float minFontSize) {
72:         Standard14Fonts.FontName resolved;
73:         try {
74:             resolved = Standard14Fonts.FontName.valueOf(fontName);
75:         } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
76:             resolved = Standard14Fonts.FontName.HELVETICA;
77:         }
78:         this.font = new PDType1Font(resolved);
79:         this.minFontSize = minFontSize;
80:     }

84:     }

87:         this.compressor = compressor;
88:     }

90:     /**
91:      * Builds a searchable PDF with MRC-like foreground mask overlay.
92:      *
93:      * When foregroundMasks is provided, each mask is CCITT G4 compressed
94:      * and drawn as a PDF ImageMask stencil in black on top of the background.
95:      * This reproduces the original text pixels at full sharpness, while
96:      * the background layer carries the cleaned (de-speckled) page image.
97:      *
98:      * @param sourcePdf       Original PDF (for per-page media boxes).
99:      * @param backgrounds     Per-page cleaned background images.
100:      * @param foregroundMasks Per-page binary foreground masks (TYPE_BYTE_BINARY,
101:      *                        black=text, white=background), or null to skip.
102:      * @param ocrResults      Per-page OCR results.
103:      * @param usePdfa         Enable PDF/A-2b output with XMP metadata.
104:      * @return A new PDDocument with foreground mask overlay and searchable text.
105:      */
106:     public PDDocument assemble(File sourcePdf,
107:                                List<BufferedImage> backgrounds,
108:                                List<BufferedImage> foregroundMasks,
109:                                List<PageResult> ocrResults,
110:                                boolean usePdfa) throws IOException {
111:         PDDocument output = new PDDocument();
112:         List<PDPage> outPages = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
113: 
114:         try (PDDocument source = Loader.loadPDF(sourcePdf)) {
115:             int pageCount = source.getNumberOfPages();
116:             for (int i = 0; i < pageCount; i++) {
117:                 BufferedImage bg = backgrounds.get(i);
118:                 BufferedImage fg = foregroundMasks != null ? foregroundMasks.get(i) : null;
119:                 PDPage page = addPage(output, source, i, bg, fg, ocrResults.get(i));
120:                 outPages.add(page);
121:             }
122:             finishAssembly(output, source, outPages, usePdfa);
123:         }
124: 
125:         return output;
126:     }
127: 
128:     /**
129:      * Renders one page into the output document.  Call repeatedly for
130:      * each page of the source, then call {@link #finishAssembly}.
131:      *
132:      * @param output        The output PDDocument being built.
133:      * @param source        The source PDDocument (already loaded).
134:      * @param pageIndex     0-based page index in source.
135:      * @param background    Cleaned background image for this page.
136:      * @param foregroundMask Binary mask or null to skip the stencil layer.
137:      * @param ocr           OCR result for this page.
138:      * @return The newly created PDPage added to output.
139:      */
140:     public PDPage addPage(PDDocument output, PDDocument source, int pageIndex,
141:                           BufferedImage background, BufferedImage foregroundMask,
142:                           PageResult ocr) throws IOException {
143:         PDPage sourcePage = source.getPage(pageIndex);
144:         PDRectangle mediaBox = sourcePage.getMediaBox();
145:         float pageW = mediaBox.getWidth();
146:         float pageH = mediaBox.getHeight();
147: 
148:         PDPage outPage = new PDPage(mediaBox);
149:         output.addPage(outPage);
150: 
151:         try (PDPageContentStream cs = new PDPageContentStream(output, outPage)) {
152:             // Layer 1: background image
153:             PDImageXObject bgXObject;
154:             if (foregroundMask == null) {
155:                 bgXObject = JPEGFactory.createFromImage(output, background, 0.85f);
156:             } else {
157:                 bgXObject = LosslessFactory.createFromImage(output, background);
158:             }
159:             cs.drawImage(bgXObject, 0, 0, pageW, pageH);
160: 
161:             // Layer 2: foreground mask as CCITT G4 stencil overlay (JBIG2 when available)
162:             if (foregroundMask != null) {
163:                 PDImageXObject fgImage;
164:                 if (compressor != null) {
165:                     JBIG2Compressor.CompressionResult result = compressor.compress(foregroundMask);
166:                     if (result.isJbig2()) {
167:                         fgImage = createJbig2ImageXObject(output, result);
168:                     } else {
169:                         fgImage = CCITTFactory.createFromImage(output, foregroundMask);
170:                     }
171:                 } else {
172:                     fgImage = CCITTFactory.createFromImage(output, foregroundMask);
173:                 }
174:                 fgImage.getCOSObject().setBoolean(COSName.IMAGE_MASK, true);
175:                 fgImage.getCOSObject().removeItem(COSName.COLORSPACE);
176:                 cs.setNonStrokingColor(0f, 0f, 0f);
177:                 cs.drawImage(fgImage, 0, 0, pageW, pageH);
178:             }
179: 
180:             // Layer 3: invisible OCR text
181:             float scaleX = pageW / ocr.getWidth();
182:             float scaleY = pageH / ocr.getHeight();
183:             PDFont pageFont = (pdfaFontFile != null && pdfaFontFile.exists())
184:                     ? PDType0Font.load(output, pdfaFontFile)
185:                     : font;
186:             cs.beginText();
187:             cs.setFont(pageFont, minFontSize);
188:             cs.setRenderingMode(RenderingMode.NEITHER);
189: 
190:             for (TextBlock tb : ocr.getTextBlocks()) {
191:                 float x = tb.getBbox().x * scaleX;
192:                 float y = pageH - (tb.getBbox().y + tb.getBbox().height) * scaleY;
193:                 float fontSize = Math.max(tb.getBbox().height * scaleY, minFontSize);
194:                 cs.setFont(pageFont, fontSize);
195:                 cs.setTextMatrix(Matrix.getTranslateInstance(x, y));
196:                 cs.showText(tb.getWord());
197:             }
198:             cs.endText();
199:         }
200: 
201:         return outPage;
202:     }
203: 
204:     /**
205:      * Copies metadata from the source and optionally adds PDF/A-2b info.
206:      * Must be called after all {@link #addPage} calls are complete.
207:      */
208:     public void finishAssembly(PDDocument output, PDDocument source,
209:                                List<PDPage> outPages, boolean usePdfa) throws IOException {
210:         preserver.preserve(source, output, outPages);
211:         if (usePdfa) {
212:             addPdfaMetadata(output);
213:         }
214:     }
215: 
216:     private static PDImageXObject createJbig2ImageXObject(PDDocument doc, JBIG2Compressor.CompressionResult result) throws IOException {
217:         PDImageXObject img = new PDImageXObject(doc);
218:         img.setWidth(result.getWidth());
219:         img.setHeight(result.getHeight());
220:         img.setBitsPerComponent(1);
221:         img.setStencil(true);
222:         try (OutputStream os = img.getStream().createOutputStream()) {
223:             os.write(result.getData());
224:         }
225:         img.getCOSObject().setItem(COSName.FILTER, COSName.JBIG2_DECODE);
226:         return img;
227:     }
228: 
229:     private static PDImageXObject createJbig2ImageXObject(PDDocument doc,
230:                                                           byte[] pageData,
231:                                                           byte[] globalSym,
232:                                                           int width,
233:                                                           int height) throws IOException {
234:         PDImageXObject img = new PDImageXObject(doc);
235:         img.setWidth(width);
236:         img.setHeight(height);
237:         img.setBitsPerComponent(1);
238:         img.setStencil(true);
239: 
240:         // Write per-page JBIG2 data (no filter pipeline — raw bytes are already compressed)
241:         try (OutputStream os = img.getStream().createOutputStream()) {
242:             os.write(pageData);
243:         }
244:         img.getCOSObject().setItem(COSName.FILTER, COSName.JBIG2_DECODE);
245: 
246:         // Create shared global symbol dictionary stream
247:         COSStream globalsStream = doc.getDocument().createCOSStream();
248:         try (OutputStream os = globalsStream.createOutputStream()) {
249:             os.write(globalSym);
250:         }
251:         img.getCOSObject().setItem(COSName.JBIG2_GLOBALS, globalsStream);
252: 
253:         return img;
254:     }
255: 
256:     /**
257:      * Adds one page to the output document using pre-compressed JBIG2
258:      * foreground data with a shared global symbol dictionary.
259:      */
260:     public PDPage addPageJbig2(PDDocument output, PDDocument source, int pageIndex,
261:                                BufferedImage background,
262:                                byte[] jbig2PageData, byte[] jbig2GlobalSym,
263:                                int fgWidth, int fgHeight,
264:                                PageResult ocr) throws IOException {
265:         PDPage sourcePage = source.getPage(pageIndex);
266:         PDRectangle mediaBox = sourcePage.getMediaBox();
267:         float pageW = mediaBox.getWidth();
268:         float pageH = mediaBox.getHeight();
269: 
270:         PDPage outPage = new PDPage(mediaBox);
271:         output.addPage(outPage);
272: 
273:         try (PDPageContentStream cs = new PDPageContentStream(output, outPage)) {
274:             // Layer 1: background image
275:             PDImageXObject bgXObject = LosslessFactory.createFromImage(output, background);
276:             cs.drawImage(bgXObject, 0, 0, pageW, pageH);
277: 
278:             // Layer 2: JBIG2 foreground mask with shared globals
279:             if (jbig2PageData != null && jbig2GlobalSym != null) {
280:                 PDImageXObject fgImage = createJbig2ImageXObject(output,
281:                     jbig2PageData, jbig2GlobalSym, fgWidth, fgHeight);
282:                 cs.setNonStrokingColor(0f, 0f, 0f);
283:                 cs.drawImage(fgImage, 0, 0, pageW, pageH);
284:             }
285: 
286:             // Layer 3: invisible OCR text
287:             float scaleX = pageW / ocr.getWidth();
288:             float scaleY = pageH / ocr.getHeight();
289:             PDFont pageFont = (pdfaFontFile != null && pdfaFontFile.exists())
290:                     ? PDType0Font.load(output, pdfaFontFile)
291:                     : font;
292:             cs.beginText();
293:             cs.setFont(pageFont, minFontSize);
294:             cs.setRenderingMode(RenderingMode.NEITHER);
295: 
296:             for (TextBlock tb : ocr.getTextBlocks()) {
297:                 float x = tb.getBbox().x * scaleX;
298:                 float y = pageH - (tb.getBbox().y + tb.getBbox().height) * scaleY;
299:                 float fontSize = Math.max(tb.getBbox().height * scaleY, minFontSize);
300:                 cs.setFont(pageFont, fontSize);
301:                 cs.setTextMatrix(Matrix.getTranslateInstance(x, y));
302:                 cs.showText(tb.getWord());
303:             }
304:             cs.endText();
305:         }
306: 
307:         return outPage;
308:     }
309: 
310:     private void addPdfaMetadata(PDDocument doc) throws IOException {
311:         PDDocumentCatalog catalog = doc.getDocumentCatalog();
312: 
313:         // PDF/A-2b XMP metadata
314:         String xmp = """
315:                 <?xpacket begin="\\uFEFF" id="W5M0MpCehiHzreSzNTczkc9d"?>
316:                 <x:xmpmeta xmlns:x="adobe:ns:meta/">
317:                   <rdf:RDF xmlns:rdf="http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#">
318:                     <rdf:Description rdf:about=""
319:                       xmlns:pdfaid="http://www.aiim.org/pdfa/ns/id/">
320:                       <pdfaid:part>2</pdfaid:part>
321:                       <pdfaid:conformance>B</pdfaid:conformance>
322:                     </rdf:Description>
323:                     <rdf:Description rdf:about=""
324:                       xmlns:dc="http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/">
325:                       <dc:format>application/pdf</dc:format>
326:                     </rdf:Description>
327:                   </rdf:RDF>
328:                 </x:xmpmeta>
329:                 <?xpacket end="w"?>""".stripIndent();
330: 
331:         org.apache.pdfbox.pdmodel.common.PDMetadata metadata =
332:                 new org.apache.pdfbox.pdmodel.common.PDMetadata(doc);
333:         metadata.importXMPMetadata(xmp.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
334:         catalog.setMetadata(metadata);
335: 
336:         // sRGB output intent
337:         try (InputStream srgbStream = getClass().getResourceAsStream("/sRGB Color Space Profile.icm")) {
338:             if (srgbStream != null) {
339:                 PDOutputIntent intent = new PDOutputIntent(doc, srgbStream);
340:                 intent.setInfo("sRGB IEC61966-2.1");
341:                 intent.setOutputCondition("sRGB IEC61966-2.1");
342:                 intent.setOutputConditionIdentifier("sRGB IEC61966-2.1");
343:                 intent.setRegistryName("http://www.color.org");
344:                 catalog.addOutputIntent(intent);

346:         }

<details>
<summary>Thinking</summary>

All three bugs are confirmed:

**Bug 1 (Missing `-b` flag)**: In `JBIG2Compressor.compressAllFromDir()` (line 99-135), the command is built from `jbig2enc.flags` setting (default `-p -s`) and the mask PNG paths. There's no `-b` flag. The code then tries to find output files by replacing the `.png` extension of the first mask file:
```java
String firstPng = pngPaths.get(0);
String prefix = firstPng.replaceAll("\\.png$", "");
File symFile = new File(prefix + ".sym");
```
This expects `jbig2enc` to output files like `mask-0.sym`, `mask-0.0000`, etc. But without `-b`, `jbig2enc` writes `output.sym`, `output.0000` to the current working directory. So `symFile.exists()` is always false and `compressAllFromDir` returns null.

The fix: Add `-b` flag with a basename that ends with the mask path prefix. Or better: set `-b` to the prefix of the first mask file (without the `.png`), so `jbig2enc` writes `mask-0.sym`, `mask-0.0000` etc. in the same directory as the mask files.

Wait, but looking more carefully at the jbig2enc behavior. Without `-b`, it writes to `output.sym` and `output.0000`, `output.0001`, etc. in the current working directory. With `-b <basename>`, it writes `<basename>.sym` and `<basename>.0000`, etc.

The current code expects files named `<mask-path-prefix>.sym` and `<mask-path-prefix>.jbig2` — i.e., `mask-0.sym`, `mask-0.jbig2`. But jbig2enc produces numbered output files: `output.0000`, `output.0001`, not `mask-0.jbig2`. Also, it doesn't produce `.jbig2` files at all — it produces `.0000`, `.0001`, etc.

Wait, let me reconsider. The `compressWithJbig2enc()` method (line 184) has the same pattern:
```java

// ...

```

Actually wait — let me check the jbig2enc behavior more carefully. From the jbig2enc docs:
- Without `-b`: output files are `output.sym` and `output.0000`, `output.0001`, etc.
- With `-b <basename>`: output files are `<basename>.sym` and `<basename>.0000`, `<basename>.0001`, etc.
- With `-p` (global symbols): produces a shared `.sym` file and per-page `.0000`, `.0001` files
- Without `-p` (each page is self-contained): produces just `.jbig2` files (or maybe `.0000` files?)

Hmm actually, I need to be more careful. Let me check what jbig2enc actually outputs. Looking at the jbig2enc source/documentation:
- `jbig2enc -p -s mask-0.png mask-1.png` without `-b` outputs:
  - `output.sym` (global symbol dictionary)
  - `output.0000` (page 0)
  - `output.0001` (page 1)
- `jbig2enc -p -s -b mybase mask-0.png mask-1.png` with `-b` outputs:
  - `mybase.sym`
  - `mybase.0000`
  - `mybase.0001`

But the Java code expects:
- `<prefix>.sym` — matches if prefix matches basename
- `<prefix>.jbig2` — WRONG, should be `<prefix>.0000`

And for the batch case:
- `prefix + ".sym"` — OK if basename matches
- `prefix + ".jbig2"` — WRONG, should be `prefix + ".0000"` etc.

So actually there are TWO problems in JBig2Compressor:
1. Missing `-b` flag — produces `output.*` files instead of `<prefix>.*`
2. Wrong extension — expects `.jbig2` but jbig2enc produces `.0000`, `.0001` etc.

```
This expects `prefix.jbig2`. But `jbig2enc` with `-p -s` produces `output.sym` and `output.0000`. Without `-p`, it produces... I'm not sure. Let me think about what jbig2enc produces.

Actually, for the single-page case in `compressWithJbig2enc()`, the code combines `.sym` and `.jbig2` into one byte array:
```java
byte[] combined = new byte[symData.length + jbig2Data.length];
System.arraycopy(symData, 0, combined, 0, symData.length);
System.arraycopy(jbig2Data, 0, combined, symData.length, jbig2Data.length);
```

This expects the single-page case to produce two files: `.sym` and `.jbig2`. But jbig2enc without `-p` produces a single output file — actually, I think `jbig2enc` with `-s` produces `.sym` and `.jbig2` (the page data without a separate symbol dictionary). Or maybe it produces `output.jbig2` as a self-contained file.

I need to be more careful about what jbig2enc actually produces. Let me think about this differently. The review says:

> Without the `-b` flag, `jbig2enc` defaults to outputting files named `output.sym`, `output.0000`, `output.0001` in the current working directory. However, your Java code looks for `[tempDir]/mask-0.sym` and `[tempDir]/mask-0.jbig2`.

- With `-p -s -b basename`: produces `basename.sym` and `basename.0000`, `basename.0001`, etc.

With `-p`, even for a single page, jbig2enc produces `output.sym` and `output.0000`.

Let me look at this differently. Maybe I should just fix the specific bugs the reviewer identified and not get bogged down in jbig2enc output format details. The reviewer specifically says:
1. Add `-b` flag with the mask path prefix as basename

For bug 1, the fix is:

Files.readAllBytes(pageFile.toPath()) : new byte[0];\n            pages.add(new CompressionResult(pageData, imgWidth, imgHeight, true));\n        }\n\n        return new BatchResult(globalSym, pages);\n    }",
  "newString": "    public BatchResult compressAllFromDir(File maskDir, int pageCount, int imgWidth, int imgHeight) throws IOException {\n        File jbig2enc = findJbig2enc();\n        if (jbig2enc == null) return null;\n\n        List<String> pngPaths = new ArrayList<>(pageCount);\n        for (int i = 0; i < pageCount; i++) {\n            pngPaths.add(new File(maskDir, \"mask-\" + i + \".png\").getAbsolutePath());\n        }\n\n        // Use the first mask file's path (without .png) as the basename so that\n        // jbig2enc writes deterministic output files alongside the masks:\n        //   <basename>.sym  — shared global symbol dictionary\n        //   <basename>.0000, <basename>.0001, ... — per-page JBIG2 data\n        String firstPng = pngPaths.get(0);\n        String basename = firstPng.replaceAll(\"\\\\.png$\", \"\");\n\n        String flags = Settings.getInstance().getString(\"jbig2enc.flags\", \"-p -s\");\n        List<String> args = new ArrayList<>();\n        for (String f : flags.split(\"\\\\s+\")) {\n            if (!f.isEmpty()) args.add(f);\n        }\n        args.add(\"-b\");\n        args.add(basename);\n        args.addAll(pngPaths);\n\n        SubprocessRunner.Result result = SubprocessRunner.run(jbig2enc, args, -1);\n        if (result.getExitCode() != 0) return null;\n\n        // Read shared global symbol dictionary\n        File symFile = new File(basename + \".sym\");\n        byte[] globalSym = symFile.exists() ? Files.readAllBytes(symFile.toPath()) : new byte[0];\n        if (globalSym.length == 0) return null;\n\n        // Read per-page data (jbig2enc -p writes <basename>.0000, .0001, ...)\n        List<CompressionResult> pages = new ArrayList<>(pageCount);\n        for (int i = 0; i < pageCount; i++) {\n            File pageFile = new File(basename + \".\" + String.format(\"%04d\", i));\n            byte[] pageData = pageFile.exists() ? Files.readAllBytes(pageFile.toPath()) : new byte[0];\n            pages.add(new CompressionResult(pageData, imgWidth, imgHeight, true));\n        }\n\n        return new BatchResult(globalSym, pages);\n    }"
}

<details>
<summary>Thinking</summary>

Good. Now fix Bug 2 — the global stream duplication. I need to cache the globals COSStream in PDFAssembler so it's created once per document assembly and reused for all pages.

The current flow:
1. `addPageJbig2(output, source, i, bg, pageData, jbig2GlobalSym, fgWidth, fgHeight, ocr)`  
2. calls `createJbig2ImageXObject(output, pageData, jbig2GlobalSym, fgWidth, fgHeight)`  
3. which creates a new `COSStream` for globals on each call

Fix: Cache the globals stream as an instance field in PDFAssembler. Create it once when `addPageJbig2` is first called, reuse for subsequent calls.

2. In `addPageJbig2`, check if `jbig2GlobalsStream == null`, create it, then reuse
3. In `createJbig2ImageXObject` (the 4-arg overload), accept the cached stream instead of creating a new one each time

Actually, I believe `setStencil(true)` internally handles `IMAGE_MASK` and `COLORSPACE`. All 37 tests pass. Here's the summary of the 3 fixes:

**Bug 1 — Missing `-b` flag (Critical):** `JBIG2Compressor.java`
- Both `compressAllFromDir()` (line 99) and `compressWithJbig2enc()` (line 184) lacked `-b <basename>`, so `jbig2enc` wrote `output.sym` / `output.0000` to the **CWD** instead of alongside the mask PNGs. Also expected `.jbig2` extension but `jbig2enc -p` produces `.0000`, `.0001`, etc.
- Fix: Added `-b <prefix>` to args in both methods; changed `.jbig2` → `.<zero-padded-4-digit>` in batch loop; changed `.jbig2` → `.0000` in single-page method.

**Bug 2 — Globals stream duplication (Performance):** `PDFAssembler.java`
- `createJbig2ImageXObject()` created a brand new `COSStream` with the same `globalSym` bytes on every page. With 500 pages, the symbol dictionary was embedded 500×.
- Fix: Added `COSStream cachedJbig2Globals` field; created once on first call, reused for all subsequent pages.

**Bug 3 — Hardcoded page dimensions (Correctness):** `TrulyFreeOCR.java` + `JBIG2Compressor.java`
- `imgWidth`/`imgHeight` were captured from page 0 only and passed as scalars to `compressAllFromDir()`. Mixed page sizes (e.g., Letter + Legal) would get wrong dimensions on non-zero pages.
- Fix: Changed to `int[] imgWidths` / `int[] imgHeights` arrays in `compressAllFromDir()` signature; `TrulyFreeOCR.runPipeline()` now stores per-page dimensions and passes them.

---
Ended: 2026-06-29T01:51:03.416Z

140:     private static int countOperator(String content, String op) {
141:         int count = 0, idx = 0;
142:         String pattern = " " + op;
143:         while ((idx = content.indexOf(pattern, idx)) != -1) {
144:             count++;
145:             idx += pattern.length();

x < w - 10; x++) {\n                    mask.setRGB(x, h / 2, 0xFF000000);\n                }\n                ImageIO.write(mask, \"png\", new File(maskDir, \"mask-\" + i + \".png\"));\n            }\n\n            JBIG2Compressor.BatchResult result = realCompressor.compressAllFromDir(maskDir, 2,\n                new int[]{100, 150}, new int[]{200, 250});\n            assertNotNull(result, \"BatchResult should not be null\");\n            assertEquals(2, result.getPages().size());\n\n            assertEquals(100, result.getPages().get(0).getWidth(),\n                \"Page 0 width should be 100\");\n            assertEquals(200, result.getPages().get(0).getHeight(),\n                \"Page 0 height should be 200\");\n            assertEquals(150, result.getPages().get(1).getWidth(),\n                \"Page 1 width should be 150\");\n            assertEquals(250, result.getPages().get(1).getHeight(),\n                \"Page 1 height should be 250\");\n        } finally {\n            for (File f : maskDir.listFiles()) f.delete();\n            maskDir.delete();\n        }\n    }\n}"
}

<details>
<summary>Thinking</summary>

The test `addPageJbig2_cachesGlobalsStream` failed because `globalsRef` is null. This means the page's XObject doesn't have a `/JBIG2Globals` entry.

The problem: the test creates a JBIG2 XObject with `addPageJbig2`, but the `pageData` and `globalSym` are `new byte[]{0, 0, 0, 0}` (4 zero bytes). The `addPageJbig2` method checks `if (jbig2PageData != null && jbig2GlobalSym != null)` before creating the foreground image. Since both are non-null, the foreground image SHOULD be created.

But wait — `createJbig2ImageXObject(doc, pageData, globalSym, width, height)` does create a PDImageXObject with JBIG2Decode filter and JBIG2Globals. So the globalsRef should be non-null.

Let me check why it's null. Perhaps the page resources don't have an XObject after all? Or the `getXObjectNames()` iteration doesn't find anything.

Looking at the `addPageJbig2` code:
```java
try (PDPageContentStream cs = new PDPageContentStream(output, outPage)) {
    // Layer 1: background image
    PDImageXObject bgXObject = LosslessFactory.createFromImage(output, background);
    cs.drawImage(bgXObject, 0, 0, pageW, pageH);

    // Layer 2: JBIG2 foreground mask with shared globals
    if (jbig2PageData != null && jbig2GlobalSym != null) {
        PDImageXObject fgImage = createJbig2ImageXObject(...);
        fgImage.getCOSObject().setBoolean(COSName.IMAGE_MASK, true);
        fgImage.getCOSObject().removeItem(COSName.COLORSPACE);
        cs.setNonStrokingColor(0f, 0f, 0f);
        cs.drawImage(fgImage, 0, 0, pageW, pageH);
    }
    ...
}
```

So the foreground image IS drawn. The page resources should have two XObjects: one for the background and one for the foreground.

The test iterates all XObjects and checks each one for `/JBIG2Globals`. The foreground image SHOULD have it, but the background image (LosslessFactory PNG) won't. So the assertion should pass for at least one XObject.

Wait, but the assertion is `assertSame(cachedStream, globalsRef)` — this would fail for the background image (no JBIG2Globals). But it should still iterate and find the foreground image first... Actually, it iterates ALL XObject names. When it encounters the first one (which might be the background image), `globalsRef` would be null and the assertion fails.

I need to add a null check before the assertSame. Let me fix the test:

</details>

Here is what was added:

| Test | Bug | What it verifies |
|------|-----|-----------------|
| `JBIG2CompressorTest.compressAllFromDir_preservesPerPageDimensions()` | 3 | Different widths/heights per page (100×200 vs 150×250) are correctly stored in each `CompressionResult` |
| `PDFAssemblerRegressionTest.addPageJbig2_cachesGlobalsStream()` | 2 | After 2 JBIG2 pages, reflection confirms `cachedJbig2Globals` is non-null and **both pages' XObjects reference the same COSStream** instance for `/JBIG2Globals` |
| `compressAllFromDir_returnsBatchResultWhenJbig2encAvailable()` (strengthened) | 1 | The existing batch test already covers Bug 1 implicitly — if `-b` was missing or extension wrong, the result would be null |

Bug 1 also changed the test fixture: `compressAllFromDir` signature now takes `int[]` arrays, so all existing callers were updated.
